<p>The <b>British Overseas Territories</b> (<b>BOTs</b>) or <b>United Kingdom Overseas Territories</b> (<b>UKOTs</b>) are fourteen <a href="/wiki/Dependent_territory" title="Dependent territory">territories</a> under the jurisdiction and sovereignty of the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-fco_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-fco-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> They are remnants of the <a href="/wiki/British_Empire" title="British Empire">British Empire</a> that have not been granted independence or have voted to remain British territories. These territories do not form part of the United Kingdom and, with the exception of <a href="/wiki/Gibraltar" title="Gibraltar">Gibraltar</a>, are not part of the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a>. Most of the permanently inhabited territories are internally self-governing, with the UK retaining responsibility for defence and <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations" title="Foreign relations">foreign relations</a>. Three are inhabited only by a transitory population of military or scientific personnel. They all share the <a href="/wiki/Monarchy_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Monarchy of the United Kingdom">British monarch</a> (<a href="/wiki/Elizabeth_II" title="Elizabeth II">Elizabeth II</a>) as <a href="/wiki/Head_of_state" title="Head of state">head of state</a>.
</p><p>As of April 2018<sup class="plainlinks noexcerpt noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit">&#91;update&#93;</a></sup> the Minister responsible for the Territories excluding the <a href="/wiki/Falkland_Islands" title="Falkland Islands">Falkland Islands</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gibraltar" title="Gibraltar">Gibraltar</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Akrotiri_and_Dhekelia" title="Akrotiri and Dhekelia">Sovereign Base Areas of Akrotiri and Dhekelia</a> on <a href="/wiki/Cyprus" title="Cyprus">Cyprus</a>, is the <a href="/wiki/Foreign_and_Commonwealth_Office#Ministers" title="Foreign and Commonwealth Office">Minister of State for the Commonwealth and the UN</a>. The other three territories are the responsibility of the <a href="/wiki/Minister_of_State_for_Europe" title="Minister of State for Europe">Minister of State for Europe and the Americas</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Current_overseas_territories">Current overseas territories</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Current overseas territories">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The fourteen British Overseas Territories are:<sup id="cite_ref-collections.europarchive.org_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-collections.europarchive.org-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Map">Map</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Map">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:752px;"><a href="/wiki/File:British_Overseas.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/British_Overseas.png/750px-British_Overseas.png" decoding="async" width="750" height="620" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/British_Overseas.png/1125px-British_Overseas.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/British_Overseas.png/1500px-British_Overseas.png 2x" data-file-width="2768" data-file-height="2288" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:British_Overseas.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #FF5050; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;British Overseas Territories</div> <div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #66FF66; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;United Kingdom</div> <div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #3399FF; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Crown_dependencies" title="Crown dependencies">Crown dependencies</a></div></div></div></div></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Collective_titles">Collective titles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Collective titles">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_the_British_Overseas_Territories_(unofficial).svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/Flag_of_the_British_Overseas_Territories_%28unofficial%29.svg/220px-Flag_of_the_British_Overseas_Territories_%28unofficial%29.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="110" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/Flag_of_the_British_Overseas_Territories_%28unofficial%29.svg/330px-Flag_of_the_British_Overseas_Territories_%28unofficial%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/Flag_of_the_British_Overseas_Territories_%28unofficial%29.svg/440px-Flag_of_the_British_Overseas_Territories_%28unofficial%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="300" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_the_British_Overseas_Territories_(unofficial).svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Unofficial flag for the overseas territories used by <i><a href="/wiki/Friends_of_the_British_Overseas_Territories" title="Friends of the British Overseas Territories">Friends of the British Overseas Territories</a></i>, a charitable organisation.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup></div></div></div>

<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ed/Flag_of_South_Georgia_and_the_South_Sandwich_Islands.svg/23px-Flag_of_South_Georgia_and_the_South_Sandwich_Islands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ed/Flag_of_South_Georgia_and_the_South_Sandwich_Islands.svg/35px-Flag_of_South_Georgia_and_the_South_Sandwich_Islands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ed/Flag_of_South_Georgia_and_the_South_Sandwich_Islands.svg/46px-Flag_of_South_Georgia_and_the_South_Sandwich_Islands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="750" data-file-height="375" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/South_Georgia_and_the_South_Sandwich_Islands" title="South Georgia and the South Sandwich Islands">South Georgia and the South Sandwich Islands</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Flag_of_the_Turks_and_Caicos_Islands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Turks_and_Caicos_Islands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Flag_of_the_Turks_and_Caicos_Islands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Turks_and_Caicos_Islands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Flag_of_the_Turks_and_Caicos_Islands.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_Turks_and_Caicos_Islands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Turks_and_Caicos_Islands" title="Turks and Caicos Islands">Turks and Caicos Islands</a></li></ul>
<hr />

<a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg" class="image"><img alt="Flag of the United Kingdom.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/32px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="16" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/48px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/64px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" /></a> <a href="/wiki/Portal:United_Kingdom" title="Portal:United Kingdom">United Kingdom&#32;portal</a>  <div class="hlist" style="text-align:center;font-weight:normal;">

<li><a href="https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Atlas_of_the_United_Kingdom" class="extiw" title="commons:Atlas of the United Kingdom">Atlas</a></li></ul>
</div></td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:right;font-size:115%;padding-top: 0.6em;"><div class="plainlinks hlist navbar mini"><ul><li class="nv-view"><a href="/wiki/Template:Politics_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Template:Politics of the United Kingdom"><abbr title="View this template">v</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-talk"><a href="/wiki/Template_talk:Politics_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Template talk:Politics of the United Kingdom"><abbr title="Discuss this template">t</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-edit"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:Politics_of_the_United_Kingdom&amp;action=edit"><abbr title="Edit this template">e</abbr></a></li></ul></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The term "British Overseas Territory" was introduced by the <a href="/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories_Act_2002" title="British Overseas Territories Act 2002">British Overseas Territories Act 2002</a>, replacing the term <i>British Dependent Territory</i>, introduced by the <a href="/wiki/British_Nationality_Act_1981" title="British Nationality Act 1981">British Nationality Act 1981</a>. Prior to 1 January 1983, the territories were officially referred to as <i><a href="/wiki/Crown_colony" title="Crown colony">British Crown Colonies</a></i>.
</p><p>Although the <a href="/wiki/Crown_dependencies" title="Crown dependencies">Crown dependencies</a> of <a href="/wiki/Jersey" title="Jersey">Jersey</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bailiwick_of_Guernsey" title="Bailiwick of Guernsey">Guernsey</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Isle_of_Man" title="Isle of Man">Isle of Man</a> are also under the <a href="/wiki/Sovereignty" title="Sovereignty">sovereignty</a> of the British monarch, they are in a different constitutional relationship with the United Kingdom.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> The British Overseas Territories and Crown Dependencies are themselves distinct from the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_realm" title="Commonwealth realm">Commonwealth realms</a>, a group of 16 independent countries (including the United Kingdom) each having Elizabeth II as their reigning monarch, and from the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Nations" title="Commonwealth of Nations">Commonwealth of Nations</a>, a voluntary association of 53 countries mostly with historic links to the British Empire (which also includes all Commonwealth realms).
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Population">Population</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Population">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>With the exceptions of the <a href="/wiki/British_Antarctic_Territory" title="British Antarctic Territory">British Antarctic Territory</a> and <a href="/wiki/South_Georgia_and_the_South_Sandwich_Islands" title="South Georgia and the South Sandwich Islands">South Georgia and the South Sandwich Islands</a> (which host only officials and research station staff) and the <a href="/wiki/British_Indian_Ocean_Territory" title="British Indian Ocean Territory">British Indian Ocean Territory</a> (used as a military base), the Territories retain permanent civilian populations. Permanent residency for the approximately 7,000 civilians living in the Sovereign Base Areas of <a href="/wiki/Akrotiri_and_Dhekelia" title="Akrotiri and Dhekelia">Akrotiri and Dhekelia</a> is limited to citizens of the Republic of <a href="/wiki/Cyprus" title="Cyprus">Cyprus</a>.
</p><p>Collectively, the Territories encompass a population of about 250,000 people and a land area of about 1,727,570 square kilometres (667,020&#160;sq&#160;mi). The vast majority of this land area, 1,700,000 square kilometres (660,000&#160;sq&#160;mi), constitutes the almost uninhabited British Antarctic Territory, while the largest territory by population, Bermuda, accounts for almost a quarter of the total BOT population. At the other end of the scale, three territories have no civilian population; the Antarctic territory, the British Indian Ocean Territory (from which the Chagos Islanders were <a href="/wiki/Expulsion_of_the_Chagossians" title="Expulsion of the Chagossians">controversially removed</a>) and South Georgia. <a href="/wiki/Pitcairn_Islands" title="Pitcairn Islands">Pitcairn Islands</a>, settled by the survivors of the <a href="/wiki/Mutiny_on_the_Bounty" title="Mutiny on the Bounty">Mutiny on the Bounty</a>, is the smallest settled territory with 49 inhabitants, while the smallest by land area is Gibraltar on the southern tip of the Iberian peninsula.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> The United Kingdom participates in the <a href="/wiki/Antarctic_Treaty_System" title="Antarctic Treaty System">Antarctic Treaty System</a><sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> and, as part of a mutual agreement, the British Antarctic Territory is recognised by four of the six other <a href="/wiki/Territorial_claims_in_Antarctica" title="Territorial claims in Antarctica">sovereign nations making claims to Antarctic territory</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: History">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/British_Empire" title="British Empire">British Empire</a>, <a href="/wiki/Territorial_evolution_of_the_British_Empire" title="Territorial evolution of the British Empire">Territorial evolution of the British Empire</a>, and <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_that_have_gained_independence_from_the_United_Kingdom" title="List of countries that have gained independence from the United Kingdom">List of countries that have gained independence from the United Kingdom</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Bermuda-Harbour_and_Town_of_St_George.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Bermuda-Harbour_and_Town_of_St_George.jpg/250px-Bermuda-Harbour_and_Town_of_St_George.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="187" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Bermuda-Harbour_and_Town_of_St_George.jpg/375px-Bermuda-Harbour_and_Town_of_St_George.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3a/Bermuda-Harbour_and_Town_of_St_George.jpg 2x" data-file-width="450" data-file-height="337" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Bermuda-Harbour_and_Town_of_St_George.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/St._George%27s,_Bermuda" title="St. George&#39;s, Bermuda">St. George's</a> town, in the Islands of Bermuda, or "The Somers Isles". The colony was founded by the wrecking of the flagship of the <a href="/wiki/London_Company" title="London Company">Virginia Company</a> in 1609. The Company's charter was extended to include Bermuda in 1612, and it has remained a British colony ever since. Since the rebellion of <a href="/wiki/Virginia" title="Virginia">Virginia</a>, it has been the oldest-remaining British colony, and the town of St. George's is the oldest continuously inhabited British settlement in the New World.<sup id="cite_ref-Smithsonian_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Smithsonian-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup></div></div></div>
<p>Early colonies, in the sense of English subjects residing in lands hitherto outside the control of the English government, were generally known as "<a href="/wiki/Plantation_(settlement_or_colony)" title="Plantation (settlement or colony)">Plantations</a>".
</p><p>The first, unofficial, colony was <a href="/wiki/Newfoundland_(island)" title="Newfoundland (island)">Newfoundland</a>, where English fishermen routinely set up seasonal camps in the 16th century.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> It is now a province of Canada known as Newfoundland and Labrador. It retains strong cultural ties with Britain.
</p><p>English colonisation of North America began officially in 1607 with the settlement of <a href="/wiki/Jamestown,_Virginia" title="Jamestown, Virginia">Jamestown</a>, the first successful permanent colony in <a href="/wiki/Colony_and_Dominion_of_Virginia" class="mw-redirect" title="Colony and Dominion of Virginia">Virginia</a> (a term that was then applied generally to North America). Its offshoot, Bermuda, was settled inadvertently after the wrecking of the Virginia company's flagship there in 1609, with the <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Company" title="Virginia Company">Virginia Company</a>'s charter extended to officially include the archipelago in 1612. <a href="/wiki/St._George%27s,_Bermuda" title="St. George&#39;s, Bermuda">St. George's</a> town, founded in Bermuda in that year, remains the oldest continuously inhabited British settlement in the New World (with some historians stating that – its formation predating the 1619 conversion of "James Fort" into "Jamestown" – St. George's was actually the first successful town the English established in the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a>). Bermuda and Bermudians have played important, sometimes pivotal, but generally underestimated or unacknowledged roles in the shaping of the English and British trans-Atlantic Empires. These include maritime commerce, settlement of the continent and of the West Indies, and the projection of naval power via the colony's <a href="/wiki/Privateer" title="Privateer">privateers</a>, among other areas.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>
The growth of the <a href="/wiki/British_Empire" title="British Empire">British Empire</a> in the 19th century, to its territorial peak in the 1920s, saw Britain acquire nearly one quarter of the world's land mass, including territories with large indigenous populations in Asia and Africa. From the mid-nineteenth century to the early twentieth century, the larger settler colonies&#160;– in Canada, Australia, New Zealand and South Africa&#160;– first became <a href="/wiki/Self-governing_colony" title="Self-governing colony">self-governing colonies</a> and then achieved independence in all matters except foreign policy, defence and trade. Separate self-governing colonies federated to become Canada (in 1867), Australia (in 1901), South Africa (in 1910), and Rhodesia (in 1965). These and other large self-governing colonies had become known as <a href="/wiki/Dominion" title="Dominion">Dominions</a> by the 1920s. The Dominions achieved almost full independence with the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Westminster_1931" title="Statute of Westminster 1931">Statute of Westminster (1931)</a>.</p><div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:United_Kingdom_in_its_region_(North_America_special).svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/United_Kingdom_in_its_region_%28North_America_special%29.svg/220px-United_Kingdom_in_its_region_%28North_America_special%29.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/United_Kingdom_in_its_region_%28North_America_special%29.svg/330px-United_Kingdom_in_its_region_%28North_America_special%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/United_Kingdom_in_its_region_%28North_America_special%29.svg/440px-United_Kingdom_in_its_region_%28North_America_special%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="415" data-file-height="233" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:United_Kingdom_in_its_region_(North_America_special).svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Many of the overseas territories are in the Caribbean, as shown on the map.</div></div></div><p>Through a process of <a href="/wiki/British_Empire#Decolonisation_and_decline_(1945–1997)" title="British Empire">decolonisation</a> following the Second World War, most of the British colonies in Africa, Asia and the Caribbean gained independence. Some colonies became <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_realm" title="Commonwealth realm">Commonwealth realms</a>, retaining the British monarch as their own <a href="/wiki/Head_of_state" title="Head of state">head of state</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> Most former colonies and protectorates became <a href="/wiki/Member_states_of_the_Commonwealth_of_Nations" title="Member states of the Commonwealth of Nations">member states of the Commonwealth of Nations</a>, a non-political, <a href="/wiki/Voluntary_association" title="Voluntary association">voluntary association</a> of equal members, comprising a population of around 2.2&#160;billion people.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the independence of <a href="/wiki/Southern_Rhodesia" title="Southern Rhodesia">Southern Rhodesia</a> (now <a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe" title="Zimbabwe">Zimbabwe</a>) in Africa in 1980 and <a href="/wiki/British_Honduras" title="British Honduras">British Honduras</a> (now <a href="/wiki/Belize" title="Belize">Belize</a>) in Central America in 1981, the last major colony that remained was <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a>, with a population of over 5 million.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> With 1997 approaching, the United Kingdom and China negotiated the <a href="/wiki/Sino-British_Joint_Declaration" title="Sino-British Joint Declaration">Sino-British Joint Declaration</a>, which led to the whole of Hong Kong becoming a "<a href="/wiki/Special_administrative_region_(People%27s_Republic_of_China)" class="mw-redirect" title="Special administrative region (People&#39;s Republic of China)">special administrative region</a>" of China in 1997, subject to various conditions intended to guarantee the preservation of Hong Kong's capitalist economy and its way of life under British rule for at least <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong_Basic_Law" title="Hong Kong Basic Law">50 years after the handover</a>. <a href="/wiki/George_Town,_Cayman_Islands" title="George Town, Cayman Islands">George Town</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Cayman_Islands" title="Cayman Islands">Cayman Islands</a> has consequently become the largest city in the Overseas Territories.
</p><p>In 2002, the British Parliament passed the <a href="/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories_Act_2002" title="British Overseas Territories Act 2002">British Overseas Territories Act 2002</a>. This reclassified the UK's dependent territories as <i>overseas territories</i> and, with the exception of those people solely connected with the Sovereign Base Areas of Cyprus, restored full British citizenship to their inhabitants.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Government">Government</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Government">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:McKeeva_Bush,_Premier_of_the_Cayman_Islands_2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ef/McKeeva_Bush%2C_Premier_of_the_Cayman_Islands_2.jpg/220px-McKeeva_Bush%2C_Premier_of_the_Cayman_Islands_2.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ef/McKeeva_Bush%2C_Premier_of_the_Cayman_Islands_2.jpg/330px-McKeeva_Bush%2C_Premier_of_the_Cayman_Islands_2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ef/McKeeva_Bush%2C_Premier_of_the_Cayman_Islands_2.jpg/440px-McKeeva_Bush%2C_Premier_of_the_Cayman_Islands_2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3888" data-file-height="2592" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:McKeeva_Bush,_Premier_of_the_Cayman_Islands_2.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/McKeeva_Bush" title="McKeeva Bush">McKeeva Bush</a>, Premier of the <a href="/wiki/Cayman_Islands" title="Cayman Islands">Cayman Islands</a> in 2012</div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Head_of_state">Head of state</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Head of state">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The head of state in the overseas territories is the British monarch, Elizabeth II. The Queen's role in the territories is in her role as Queen of the United Kingdom, and not in right of each territory.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> The Queen appoints a representative in each territory to exercise her executive power. In territories with a permanent population, a Governor is appointed by the Queen on the advice of the British Government. Currently (2019) all but two Governors are either career diplomats or have worked in other Civil Service departments. The remaining two Governors are former members of the British armed forces. In territories without a permanent population, a Commissioner is usually appointed to represent the Queen. Exceptionally, in the oversea territory of Saint Helena, Ascension and Tristan da Cunha, an Administrator is appointed to be the Governor's representative in each of the two distant parts of the territory, namely <a href="/wiki/Ascension_Island" title="Ascension Island">Ascension Island</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tristan_da_Cunha" title="Tristan da Cunha">Tristan da Cunha</a>.
</p><p>The role of the Governor is to act as the <i>de facto</i> <a href="/wiki/Head_of_state" title="Head of state">head of state</a>, and they are usually responsible for appointing the head of government, and senior political positions in the territory. The Governor is also responsible for liaising with the UK Government, and carrying out any ceremonial duties. A Commissioner has the same powers as a Governor, but also acts as the head of government.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_41-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Local_government">Local government</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Local government">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/List_of_current_heads_of_government_in_the_United_Kingdom_and_dependencies#Overseas_Territories" title="List of current heads of government in the United Kingdom and dependencies">List of current heads of government in the United Kingdom and dependencies §&#160;Overseas Territories</a></div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_leaders_of_dependent_territories" title="List of leaders of dependent territories">List of leaders of dependent territories</a></div>
<p>All the overseas territories have their own system of government, and localised laws. The structure of the government appears to be closely correlated to the size and political development of the territory.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_41-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<table class="wikitable">

<tbody><tr>
<th>Territories</th>
<th>Government
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/British_Antarctic_Territory" title="British Antarctic Territory">British Antarctic Territory</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Georgia_and_the_South_Sandwich_Islands" title="South Georgia and the South Sandwich Islands">South Georgia and the South Sandwich Islands</a></li></ul>
</td>
<td>There is no native or permanent population; therefore there is no elected government. The Commissioner, supported by an Administrator, runs the affairs of the territory.
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/British_Indian_Ocean_Territory" title="British Indian Ocean Territory">British&#160;Indian&#160;Ocean&#160;Territory</a></li></ul>
</td>
<td>There is no elected government, as there is no native settled population. The <a href="/wiki/Chagossians" title="Chagossians">Chagos Islanders</a> – who were forcibly <a href="/wiki/Expulsion_of_the_Chagossians" title="Expulsion of the Chagossians"> evicted</a> from the territory in 1971 – won a <a href="/wiki/High_Court_of_Justice" title="High Court of Justice">High Court</a> Judgement allowing them to return, but this was then overridden by an <a href="/wiki/Order_in_Council" title="Order in Council">Order in Council</a> preventing them from returning. The final appeal to the <a href="/wiki/Judicial_functions_of_the_House_of_Lords" title="Judicial functions of the House of Lords">House of Lords</a> (regarding the lawfulness of the Order in Council) was decided in the government's favour, exhausting the islanders' legal options in the United Kingdom at present.
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Akrotiri_and_Dhekelia" title="Akrotiri and Dhekelia">Akrotiri and Dhekelia</a></li></ul>
</td>
<td>There is no elected government. The Commander British Forces Cyprus acts as the territory's Administrator, with a Chief Officer responsible for day-to-day running of the civil government. As far as possible, there is convergence of laws<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Please_clarify" title="Wikipedia:Please clarify"><span title="Convergence is dynamic, but this is probably meant to refer to a static condition. Should this read &quot;... the laws are consistent with those of the Republic of Cyprus&quot; or &quot;... the laws are written to conform with those of the Republic of Cyprus&quot;? (April 2017)">clarification needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> with those of the Republic of Cyprus.
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Pitcairn_Islands" title="Pitcairn Islands">Pitcairn Islands</a></li></ul>
</td>
<td>There are an elected <a href="/wiki/List_of_rulers_of_the_Pitcairn_Islands" title="List of rulers of the Pitcairn Islands">Mayor</a> and <a href="/wiki/Island_Council_(Pitcairn)" title="Island Council (Pitcairn)">Island Council</a>, who have the power to propose and administer local legislation. However, their decisions are subject to approval by the Governor, who retains near-unlimited powers of plenary legislation on behalf of the United Kingdom Government.
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Falkland_Islands" title="Falkland Islands">Falkland Islands</a></li></ul>
</td>
<td>The Government consists of an elected <a href="/wiki/Legislative_Assembly_of_the_Falkland_Islands" title="Legislative Assembly of the Falkland Islands">Legislative Assembly</a>, with the <a href="/wiki/Chief_Executive_of_the_Falkland_Islands" title="Chief Executive of the Falkland Islands">Chief Executive</a> and the Director of Corporate Resources as <i><a href="/wiki/Ex_officio" class="mw-redirect" title="Ex officio">ex officio</a></i> members.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Saint_Helena,_Ascension_and_Tristan_da_Cunha" title="Saint Helena, Ascension and Tristan da Cunha">Saint Helena, Ascension and Tristan da Cunha</a></li></ul>
</td>
<td>The Government consists of an elected Legislative Council. The Governor is the head of government and leads the Executive Council, consisting of appointed members made up from the Legislative Council and two <i>ex-officio</i> members. Governance on Ascension Island and Tristan da Cunha is led by Administrators who are advised by elected Island Councils.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Anguilla" title="Anguilla">Anguilla</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/British_Virgin_Islands" title="British Virgin Islands">British Virgin Islands</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cayman_Islands" title="Cayman Islands">Cayman Islands</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Montserrat" title="Montserrat">Montserrat</a></li></ul>
</td>
<td>These territories have a House of Assembly, Legislative Assembly (Cayman Islands and Montserrat), with political parties. The Executive Council is usually called a cabinet and is led by a <a href="/wiki/Premier" title="Premier">Premier</a>, who is the leader of the majority party in parliament. The Governor exercises less power over local affairs and deals mostly with foreign affairs and economic issues, while the elected government controls most "domestic" concerns.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (October 2009)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Gibraltar" title="Gibraltar">Gibraltar</a></li></ul>
</td>
<td>Under the <a href="/wiki/Gibraltar_Constitution_Order_2006" title="Gibraltar Constitution Order 2006">Gibraltar Constitution Order 2006</a> which was approved in Gibraltar by <a href="/wiki/Gibraltarian_constitutional_referendum,_2006" class="mw-redirect" title="Gibraltarian constitutional referendum, 2006">a referendum</a>, Gibraltar now has a <a href="/wiki/Gibraltar_Parliament" title="Gibraltar Parliament">Parliament</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Gibraltar" title="Government of Gibraltar">Government of Gibraltar</a>, headed by the <a href="/wiki/Chief_Minister_of_Gibraltar" title="Chief Minister of Gibraltar">Chief Minister</a>, is elected. Defence, external affairs and internal security vest in the <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Gibraltar" title="Governor of Gibraltar">Governor</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Bermuda" title="Bermuda">Bermuda</a></li></ul>
</td>
<td>Bermuda, settled in 1609, and self-governed since 1620, is the oldest and most populous of the Overseas Territories. The bicameral <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Bermuda" title="Parliament of Bermuda">Parliament</a> consists of a <a href="/wiki/Senate_of_Bermuda" title="Senate of Bermuda">Senate</a> and a <a href="/wiki/House_of_Assembly_of_Bermuda" title="House of Assembly of Bermuda">House of Assembly</a>, and most executive powers have been devolved to the head of government, known as the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Premiers_of_Bermuda" title="List of Premiers of Bermuda">Premier</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Turks_and_Caicos_Islands" title="Turks and Caicos Islands">Turks and Caicos Islands</a></li></ul>
</td>
<td>The Turks and Caicos Islands adopted a new constitution effective 9 August 2006; their head of government now also has the title <a href="/wiki/Premier_of_the_Turks_and_Caicos_Islands" title="Premier of the Turks and Caicos Islands">Premier</a>, their legislature is called the House of Assembly, and their autonomy has been greatly increased.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Legal_system">Legal system</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Legal system">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox vcard" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold;background-color: #ededed"><div style="display:inline" class="fn org">British Overseas Territories Joint Ministerial Council</div></th></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;background-color: #ededed">Type</th></tr><tr><th scope="row">Type</th><td><div style="padding:0.1em 0;line-height:1.3em;"><div style="display:inline" class="category">Dialogue forum</div>  </div></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Seats</th><td>28-30</td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;background-color: #ededed">Elections</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><div style="padding:0.1em 0;line-height:1.2em;"><a href="/wiki/Electoral_system" title="Electoral system">Voting system</a></div></th><td>All members elected either as MPs in the UK cabinet or as heads of Government or Ministers in Overseas Territories.</td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;background-color: #ededed">Meeting place</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" class="label" style="text-align:center"><a href="/wiki/Westminster" title="Westminster">Westminster</a>, <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a></td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;background-color: #ededed">Website</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span class="url"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.gov.uk/government/topical-events/overseas-territories-joint-ministerial-council">www<wbr />.gov<wbr />.uk<wbr />/government<wbr />/topical-events<wbr />/overseas-territories-joint-ministerial-council</a></span></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Each overseas territory has its own legal system independent of the United Kingdom. The legal system is generally based on <a href="/wiki/English_common_law" class="mw-redirect" title="English common law">English common law</a>, with some distinctions for local circumstances. Each territory has its own attorney general, and court system. For the smaller territories, the UK may appoint a UK-based lawyer or judge to work on legal cases. This is particularly important for cases involving serious crimes and where it is impossible to find a jury who will not know the defendant in a small population island.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Pitcairn_sexual_assault_trial_of_2004" title="Pitcairn sexual assault trial of 2004">Pitcairn sexual assault trial of 2004</a> is an example of how the UK may choose to provide the legal framework for particular cases where the territory cannot do so alone.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Joint_Ministerial_Council">Joint Ministerial Council</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Joint Ministerial Council">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>A joint ministerial council of UK ministers, and the leaders of the Overseas Territories has been held annually since 2012 to provide representation between UK Government departments and Overseas Territory Governments.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Disputed_sovereignty">Disputed sovereignty</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Disputed sovereignty">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The British Indian Ocean Territory (BIOT) is the subject of a territorial dispute with <a href="/wiki/Mauritius" title="Mauritius">Mauritius</a>, whose government claim that the separation of the <a href="/wiki/Chagos_Archipelago" title="Chagos Archipelago">Chagos Archipelago</a> from the rest of <a href="/wiki/British_Mauritius" title="British Mauritius">British Mauritius</a> in 1965, three years before Mauritius was granted independence from the United Kingdom, was not lawful. The long-running dispute was referred in 2017 to the <a href="/wiki/International_Court_of_Justice" title="International Court of Justice">International Court of Justice</a>, which issued an advisory opinion on 25 February 2019 which supported the position of the Government of Mauritius.
</p><p>The British Antarctic Territory has some overlap with territorial claims by both Argentina and Chile. However, territorial claims on the continent may not currently be advanced, under the holding measures of the <a href="/wiki/Antarctic_Treaty_System" title="Antarctic Treaty System">Antarctic Treaty System</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relations_with_the_United_Kingdom">Relations with the United Kingdom</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Relations with the United Kingdom">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:British_Overseas_Territories_Joint_Ministerial_Council_with_Cameron.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/British_Overseas_Territories_Joint_Ministerial_Council_with_Cameron.jpg/250px-British_Overseas_Territories_Joint_Ministerial_Council_with_Cameron.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/British_Overseas_Territories_Joint_Ministerial_Council_with_Cameron.jpg/375px-British_Overseas_Territories_Joint_Ministerial_Council_with_Cameron.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/British_Overseas_Territories_Joint_Ministerial_Council_with_Cameron.jpg/500px-British_Overseas_Territories_Joint_Ministerial_Council_with_Cameron.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2136" data-file-height="1424" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:British_Overseas_Territories_Joint_Ministerial_Council_with_Cameron.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Leaders of the Overseas Territories with former Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a> in 2012.</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Tristanfromspace.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Tristanfromspace.jpg/250px-Tristanfromspace.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Tristanfromspace.jpg/375px-Tristanfromspace.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Tristanfromspace.jpg/500px-Tristanfromspace.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1440" data-file-height="960" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Tristanfromspace.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Tristan_da_Cunha" title="Tristan da Cunha">Tristan da Cunha</a> on 6 February 2013, as seen from space. The population was temporarily evacuated to the UK in 1961 because of an eruption. Postal code TDCU 1ZZ</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Little_Bay_Montserrat.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Little_Bay_Montserrat.jpg/250px-Little_Bay_Montserrat.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="188" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Little_Bay_Montserrat.jpg/375px-Little_Bay_Montserrat.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Little_Bay_Montserrat.jpg/500px-Little_Bay_Montserrat.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1600" data-file-height="1200" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Little_Bay_Montserrat.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Coastline at Little Bay, the site of the new capital of Montserrat replacing <a href="/wiki/Plymouth,_Montserrat" title="Plymouth, Montserrat">Plymouth</a>. The project is funded by the<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> UK's <a href="/wiki/Department_for_International_Development" title="Department for International Development">Department for International Development</a>.</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:British_Overseas_Territories_(at_the_same_geographic_scale).svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/British_Overseas_Territories_%28at_the_same_geographic_scale%29.svg/220px-British_Overseas_Territories_%28at_the_same_geographic_scale%29.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="213" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/British_Overseas_Territories_%28at_the_same_geographic_scale%29.svg/330px-British_Overseas_Territories_%28at_the_same_geographic_scale%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/British_Overseas_Territories_%28at_the_same_geographic_scale%29.svg/440px-British_Overseas_Territories_%28at_the_same_geographic_scale%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="771" data-file-height="745" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:British_Overseas_Territories_(at_the_same_geographic_scale).svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>British Overseas Territories at the same geographic scale as the UK.</div></div></div>
<p>Historically the <a href="/wiki/Secretary_of_State_for_the_Colonies" title="Secretary of State for the Colonies">Secretary of State for the Colonies</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Colonial_Office" title="Colonial Office">Colonial Office</a> were responsible for overseeing all British Colonies, but today the <a href="/wiki/Foreign_and_Commonwealth_Office" title="Foreign and Commonwealth Office">Foreign and Commonwealth Office</a> (FCO) has the responsibility of looking after the interests of all overseas territories except the Sovereign Base Areas of Akrotiri and Dhekelia, which comes under the jurisdiction of the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Defence_(United_Kingdom)" title="Ministry of Defence (United Kingdom)">Ministry of Defence</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Within the FCO, the general responsibility for the territories is handled by the Overseas Territories Directorate.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2012, the FCO published <i>The Overseas Territories: security, success and sustainability</i> which set out Britain's policy for the Overseas Territories, covering six main areas:<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Defence, security and safety of the territories and their people</li>
<li>Successful and resilient economies</li>
<li>Cherishing the environment</li>
<li>Making government work better</li>
<li>Vibrant and flourishing communities</li>
<li>Productive links with the wider world</li></ul>
<p>Britain and the overseas territories do not have diplomatic representations, although the governments of the overseas territories with indigenous populations all retain a representative office in London. The United Kingdom Overseas Territories Association (UKOTA) also represents the interests of the territories in London. The governments in both London and territories occasionally meet to mitigate or resolve disagreements over the process of governance in the territories and levels of autonomy.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Britain provides financial assistance to the overseas territories via the <a href="/wiki/Department_for_International_Development" title="Department for International Development">Department for International Development</a>. Currently<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Dates_and_numbers#Chronological_items" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers"><span title="The time period mentioned near this tag is ambiguous. (November 2010)">when?</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> only Montserrat and Saint Helena receive budgetary aid (i.e. financial contribution to recurrent funding).<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (November 2010)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> Several specialist funds are made available by the UK, including:
</p>
<ul><li>The Good Government Fund which provides assistance on government administration;</li>
<li>The Economic Diversification Programme Budget which aim to diversify and enhance the economic bases of the territories.</li></ul>
<p>The territories have no official representation in the UK Parliament, but have informal representation through the All-Party Parliamentary Group,<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> and can <a href="/wiki/Epetition" class="mw-redirect" title="Epetition">petition</a> the UK Government through the <a href="/wiki/Directgov" title="Directgov">Directgov</a> e-Petitions website.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> Only <a href="/wiki/Gibraltar" title="Gibraltar">Gibraltar</a> has representation in the <a href="/wiki/European_Parliament" title="European Parliament">European Parliament</a> and it shares its Member with the region of <a href="/wiki/South_West_England_(European_Parliament_constituency)" title="South West England (European Parliament constituency)">South West England</a>.
</p><p>Two national parties, <a href="/wiki/UKIP" class="mw-redirect" title="UKIP">UKIP</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Democrats_(UK)" title="Liberal Democrats (UK)">Liberal Democrats</a>, have endorsed calls for direct representation of overseas territories in the UK Parliament, as well as backbench members of the <a href="/wiki/Conservative_Party_(UK)" title="Conservative Party (UK)">Conservative Party</a> and <a href="/wiki/Labour_Party_(UK)" title="Labour Party (UK)">Labour Party</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Foreign_affairs">Foreign affairs</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Foreign affairs">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Special_member_state_territories_and_the_European_Union" title="Special member state territories and the European Union">Special member state territories and the European Union</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:BritishAntarcticTerritory.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/BritishAntarcticTerritory.svg/220px-BritishAntarcticTerritory.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/BritishAntarcticTerritory.svg/330px-BritishAntarcticTerritory.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/BritishAntarcticTerritory.svg/440px-BritishAntarcticTerritory.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="960" data-file-height="640" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:BritishAntarcticTerritory.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Map showing the portion of <a href="/wiki/Antarctica" title="Antarctica">Antarctica</a> claimed by the UK as <a href="/wiki/British_Antarctic_Territory" title="British Antarctic Territory">British Antarctic Territory</a>.</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Gibraltar_aerial_view_looking_northwest.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Gibraltar_aerial_view_looking_northwest.jpg/220px-Gibraltar_aerial_view_looking_northwest.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="176" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Gibraltar_aerial_view_looking_northwest.jpg/330px-Gibraltar_aerial_view_looking_northwest.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Gibraltar_aerial_view_looking_northwest.jpg/440px-Gibraltar_aerial_view_looking_northwest.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="819" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Gibraltar_aerial_view_looking_northwest.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Gibraltar is the only overseas territory included in the European Union</div></div></div>
<p>Foreign affairs of the overseas territories are handled by the FCO in London. Some territories maintain diplomatic officers in nearby countries for trade and immigration purposes. Several of the territories in the Americas maintain membership within the <a href="/wiki/Organisation_of_Eastern_Caribbean_States" title="Organisation of Eastern Caribbean States">Organisation of Eastern Caribbean States</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Community" title="Caribbean Community">Caribbean Community</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Development_Bank" title="Caribbean Development Bank">Caribbean Development Bank</a>, <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Disaster_Emergency_Management_Agency" title="Caribbean Disaster Emergency Management Agency">Caribbean Disaster Emergency Management Agency</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Association_of_Caribbean_States" title="Association of Caribbean States">Association of Caribbean States</a>. The territories are members of the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Nations" title="Commonwealth of Nations">Commonwealth of Nations</a> through the United Kingdom. The inhabited territories compete in their own right at the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_Games" title="Commonwealth Games">Commonwealth Games</a>, and three of the territories (<a href="/wiki/Bermuda" title="Bermuda">Bermuda</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Cayman_Islands" title="Cayman Islands">Cayman Islands</a> and the <a href="/wiki/British_Virgin_Islands" title="British Virgin Islands">British Virgin Islands</a>) sent teams to the <a href="/wiki/2008_Summer_Olympics" title="2008 Summer Olympics">2008 Summer Olympics</a>.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Gibraltar" title="Gibraltar">Gibraltar</a> is the only overseas territory that is part of the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> (EU), although it is not part of the European Customs Union, the European Tax Policy, the European Statistics Zone or the Common Agriculture Policy. Gibraltar is not a member of the European Union in its own right. The Sovereign Base Areas in Cyprus are not part of the European Union, but they are the only British overseas territory to use the euro as official currency. None of the other Overseas Territories are members of the EU, the main body of EU law does not apply and, although certain slices of EU law are applied to those territories as part of the EU's Association of <a href="/wiki/Overseas_Countries_and_Territories" class="mw-redirect" title="Overseas Countries and Territories">Overseas Countries and Territories</a> (OCT Association), they are not commonly enforceable in local courts. The OCT Association also provides overseas territories with structural funding for regeneration projects.
</p><p>Since the return of full <a href="/wiki/British_nationality_law" title="British nationality law">British citizenship</a><sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> to most 'belongers' of overseas territories (mainly since the <a href="/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories_Act_2002" title="British Overseas Territories Act 2002">British Overseas Territories Act 2002</a>), the citizens of those territories hold concurrent European Union citizenship, giving them rights of free movement across all EU member states.
</p><p>Five nations dispute the UK's sovereignty in the following overseas territories:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/British_Antarctic_Territory" title="British Antarctic Territory">British Antarctic Territory</a>&#160;– Territory overlaps Antarctic claims made by <a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a> and <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/British_Indian_Ocean_Territory" title="British Indian Ocean Territory">British Indian Ocean Territory</a>&#160;– claimed by <a href="/wiki/Mauritius" title="Mauritius">Mauritius</a> and <a href="/wiki/Seychelles" title="Seychelles">Seychelles</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Falkland_Islands" title="Falkland Islands">Falkland Islands</a>&#160;– claimed by <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gibraltar" title="Gibraltar">Gibraltar</a>&#160;– claimed by Spain</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Georgia_and_the_South_Sandwich_Islands" title="South Georgia and the South Sandwich Islands">South Georgia and the South Sandwich Islands</a>&#160;– claimed by <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Citizenship">Citizenship</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Citizenship">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories_citizen" title="British Overseas Territories citizen">British Overseas Territories citizen</a></div>
<p>None of the overseas territories has its own nationality status, and most residents hold two forms of <a href="/wiki/British_nationality" class="mw-redirect" title="British nationality">British nationality</a>: <a href="/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories_citizen" title="British Overseas Territories citizen">British Overseas Territories citizenship</a> (BOTC) and <a href="/wiki/British_citizenship" class="mw-redirect" title="British citizenship">British citizenship</a>. Only the latter grants the right of abode in a specific country or territory, namely, the United Kingdom proper which includes its three <a href="/wiki/Crown_Dependencies" class="mw-redirect" title="Crown Dependencies">Crown Dependencies</a>. Individual overseas territories have legislative independence over immigration, and consequently, BOTC status does not automatically grant the right of abode in any of the territories, as it depends on the territory's immigration laws. A territory may issue <a href="/wiki/Belonger_status" title="Belonger status">belonger status</a> to allow a person to reside in the territory that they have close links with. The governors of the territories may also allow naturalization of non-BOTCs as BOTCs.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Gibraltar_National_Day_011_(9719769048)_(3).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Gibraltar_National_Day_011_%289719769048%29_%283%29.jpg/220px-Gibraltar_National_Day_011_%289719769048%29_%283%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Gibraltar_National_Day_011_%289719769048%29_%283%29.jpg/330px-Gibraltar_National_Day_011_%289719769048%29_%283%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Gibraltar_National_Day_011_%289719769048%29_%283%29.jpg/440px-Gibraltar_National_Day_011_%289719769048%29_%283%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1969" data-file-height="1310" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Gibraltar_National_Day_011_(9719769048)_(3).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Thousands of <a href="/wiki/Gibraltarian_people" class="mw-redirect" title="Gibraltarian people">Gibraltarians</a> dress in their national colours of red and white during the 2013 <a href="/wiki/Gibraltar_National_Day" title="Gibraltar National Day">Gibraltar National Day</a> celebrations. Gibraltarians were the only group of overseas territories residents who could apply for full British citizenship without restrictions before 2002.</div></div></div>
<p>From 1949 to 1983, the nationality status of <a href="/wiki/CUKC" class="mw-redirect" title="CUKC">Citizenship of UK and Colonies</a> (CUKC) was shared by residents of the UK proper and residents of overseas territories, although most residents of overseas territories lost their automatic right to live in the UK after the ratification of <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_Immigrants_Act_1968" title="Commonwealth Immigrants Act 1968">Commonwealth Immigrants Act 1968</a> that year unless they were born in the UK proper or had a parent or a grandparent born in the UK.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> In 1983, CUKC status of residents of overseas territories without the right of abode in the UK was replaced by British Dependent Territories citizenship (BDTC) in the newly-minted <a href="/wiki/British_Nationality_Act_1981" title="British Nationality Act 1981">British Nationality Act 1981</a>, a status that does not come with it the right of abode in the UK or any overseas territory. For these residents, registration as full British citizens then required physical residence in the UK proper. There were only two exceptions: Falkland Islanders, who were automatically granted British citizenship and was treated as a part of the UK proper through the enactment of <a href="/wiki/British_Nationality_(Falkland_Islands)_Act_1983" title="British Nationality (Falkland Islands) Act 1983">British Nationality (Falkland Islands) Act 1983</a> due to the <a href="/wiki/Falklands_War" title="Falklands War">Falklands War</a> with Argentina, and Gibraltarians who were given the special entitlement to be registered as British citizens upon request without further conditions because of its individual membership in the <a href="/wiki/European_Economic_Area" title="European Economic Area">European Economic Area</a> and the <a href="/wiki/European_Community" class="mw-redirect" title="European Community">European Community</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>5 years after the <a href="/wiki/Handover_of_Hong_Kong" title="Handover of Hong Kong">handover of Hong Kong</a> to China in 1997, the British government amended the 1981 Act to give British citizenship without restrictions to all BDTCs (the status was also renamed BOTC at the same time) except for those solely connected with <a href="/wiki/Akrotiri_and_Dhekelia" title="Akrotiri and Dhekelia">Akrotiri and Dhekelia</a> (whose residents already held <a href="/wiki/Cypriot_citizenship" class="mw-redirect" title="Cypriot citizenship">Cypriot citizenship</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>. This restored the right of abode in the UK to residents of overseas territories after a 34-year hiatus from 1968 to 2002.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Military">Military</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Military">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Mount_Pleasant_Airport_-_Donald_Morrison.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Mount_Pleasant_Airport_-_Donald_Morrison.jpg/220px-Mount_Pleasant_Airport_-_Donald_Morrison.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Mount_Pleasant_Airport_-_Donald_Morrison.jpg/330px-Mount_Pleasant_Airport_-_Donald_Morrison.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Mount_Pleasant_Airport_-_Donald_Morrison.jpg/440px-Mount_Pleasant_Airport_-_Donald_Morrison.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3888" data-file-height="2592" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Mount_Pleasant_Airport_-_Donald_Morrison.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/RAF_Mount_Pleasant" title="RAF Mount Pleasant">RAF Mount Pleasant</a>, Falkland Islands</div></div></div>
<p>Defence of the Overseas Territories is the responsibility of the UK. Many of the overseas territories are used as military bases by the UK and its allies.
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Ascension_Island" title="Ascension Island">Ascension Island</a> (part of <a href="/wiki/Saint_Helena,_Ascension_and_Tristan_da_Cunha" title="Saint Helena, Ascension and Tristan da Cunha">Saint Helena, Ascension and Tristan da Cunha</a>) – the Base known as <a href="/wiki/RAF_Ascension_Island" title="RAF Ascension Island">RAF Ascension Island</a> is used by both the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Air_Force" title="Royal Air Force">Royal Air Force</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Air_Force" title="United States Air Force">United States Air Force</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bermuda" title="Bermuda">Bermuda</a>&#160;– became the primary <a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a> base in North America, following US independence. The Naval establishment included an admiralty, a <a href="/wiki/Royal_Naval_Dockyard,_Bermuda" title="Royal Naval Dockyard, Bermuda">dockyard</a>, and a naval squadron. A considerable <a href="/wiki/Bermuda_Garrison" title="Bermuda Garrison">military garrison</a> was built up to protect it, and Bermuda, which the British Government came to see as a base, rather than as a colony, was known as <i>Fortress Bermuda</i>, and the <i>Gibraltar of the West</i> (Bermudians, like Gibraltarians, also dub their territory "The Rock").<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> Canada and the USA also established bases in Bermuda during the Second World War, which were maintained through the <a href="/wiki/Cold_War" title="Cold War">Cold War</a>. Four air bases were located in Bermuda during the Second World War (operated by the Royal Air Force, Royal Navy, US Navy, and US Army/Army Air Force). Since 1995, the <a href="/wiki/Military_of_Bermuda" title="Military of Bermuda">military force in Bermuda</a> has been reduced to the local <a href="/wiki/Territorial_Army_(United_Kingdom)" class="mw-redirect" title="Territorial Army (United Kingdom)">territorial</a> battalion, the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Bermuda_Regiment" title="Royal Bermuda Regiment">Royal Bermuda Regiment</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/British_Indian_Ocean_Territory" title="British Indian Ocean Territory">British Indian Ocean Territory</a>&#160;– the island of <a href="/wiki/Diego_Garcia" title="Diego Garcia">Diego Garcia</a> is home to a large naval base and airbase leased to the United States by the United Kingdom until 2036 (unless renewed). There are British forces in small numbers in the BIOT for administrative and immigration purposes.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Falkland_Islands" title="Falkland Islands">Falkland Islands</a> – the <a href="/wiki/Military_of_the_Falkland_Islands" title="Military of the Falkland Islands">British Forces Falkland Islands</a> includes commitments from the <a href="/wiki/British_Army" title="British Army">British Army</a>, <a href="/wiki/Royal_Air_Force" title="Royal Air Force">Royal Air Force</a> and <a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a>, along with the <a href="/wiki/Falkland_Islands_Defence_Force" title="Falkland Islands Defence Force">Falkland Islands Defence Force</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gibraltar" title="Gibraltar">Gibraltar</a> – <a href="/wiki/British_Forces_Gibraltar" title="British Forces Gibraltar">British Forces Gibraltar</a> includes a Royal Navy <a href="/wiki/Cammell_Laird_Gibraltar" class="mw-redirect" title="Cammell Laird Gibraltar">dockyard</a> (also used by <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a>), <a href="/wiki/RAF_Gibraltar" title="RAF Gibraltar">RAF Gibraltar</a> – used by the RAF and NATO and a local garrison&#160;– the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Gibraltar_Regiment" title="Royal Gibraltar Regiment">Royal Gibraltar Regiment</a>.</li>
<li>The Sovereign Base Areas of <a href="/wiki/Akrotiri_and_Dhekelia" title="Akrotiri and Dhekelia">Akrotiri and Dhekelia</a> in Cyprus – maintained as strategic British military bases in the eastern <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean_Sea" title="Mediterranean Sea">Mediterranean Sea</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Montserrat" title="Montserrat">Montserrat</a> – the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Montserrat_Defence_Force" title="Royal Montserrat Defence Force">Royal Montserrat Defence Force</a>, historically connected with the Irish Guards, is a body of twenty volunteers, whose duties are primarily ceremonial.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Languages">Languages</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Languages">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands-113070.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands-113070.jpg/220px-Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands-113070.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands-113070.jpg/330px-Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands-113070.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands-113070.jpg/440px-Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands-113070.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2592" data-file-height="1728" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands-113070.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Cliff" title="Cliff">Cliffs</a> at <a href="/wiki/Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands" title="Gough and Inaccessible Islands">Gough and Inaccessible Islands</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>Most of the languages other than English spoken in the territories contain a large degree of English, either as a root language, or in <a href="/wiki/Codeswitching" class="mw-redirect" title="Codeswitching">codeswitching</a>, e.g. Llanito. They include:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Llanito" title="Llanito">Llanito</a> or Yanito and <a href="/wiki/Spanish_language" title="Spanish language">Spanish</a> (<a href="/wiki/Gibraltar" title="Gibraltar">Gibraltar</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cayman_Creole" class="mw-redirect" title="Cayman Creole">Cayman Creole</a> (<a href="/wiki/Cayman_Islands" title="Cayman Islands">Cayman Islands</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Turks-Caicos_Creole" class="mw-redirect" title="Turks-Caicos Creole">Turks-Caicos Creole</a> (<a href="/wiki/Turks_and_Caicos_Islands" title="Turks and Caicos Islands">Turks and Caicos Islands</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pitkern" class="mw-redirect" title="Pitkern">Pitkern</a> (<a href="/wiki/Pitcairn_Islands" title="Pitcairn Islands">Pitcairn Islands</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Greek_language" title="Greek language">Greek</a> and <a href="/wiki/Turkish_language" title="Turkish language">Turkish</a> (<a href="/wiki/Akrotiri_and_Dhekelia" title="Akrotiri and Dhekelia">Akrotiri and Dhekelia</a>)</li></ul>
<p>Forms of English:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Bermudian_English" title="Bermudian English">Bermudian English</a> (<a href="/wiki/Bermuda" title="Bermuda">Bermuda</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Falkland_Islands_English" title="Falkland Islands English">Falkland Islands English</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Currencies">Currencies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Currencies">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/List_of_British_currencies" title="List of British currencies">List of British currencies</a></div>
<p>The many British overseas territories use a varied assortment of currencies, including the euro, pound, US dollar, NZ dollar, or their own currencies, which may be pegged to one of these.
